        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

Steps to reproduce:



<span class="line"><!---->Steps to reproduce:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





1. Create a new project in GitLab or GitHub and make it public or private



<span class="line"><!---->1. Create a new project in GitLab or GitHub and make it public or private<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





2. Then in the "readme.md" paste the payload from payload.txt



<span class="line"><!---->2. Then in the "readme.md" paste the payload from payload.txt<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





3. Commit the code.



<span class="line"><!---->3. Commit the code.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





4. The payload was rendered in the browser, move your mouse over the payload.



<span class="line"><!---->4. The payload was rendered in the browser, move your mouse over the payload.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





5. Then the browser will get freeze.



<span class="line"><!---->5. Then the browser will get freeze.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





6. Check the task manager in the system and observe the memory and power usage.



<span class="line"><!---->6. Check the task manager in the system and observe the memory and power usage.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





7. For confirmation, open the GitHub link in your chrome browser and move your mouse over the "/a/a/a" or boxed markdown.



<span class="line"><!---->7. For confirmation, open the GitHub link in your chrome browser and move your mouse over the "/a/a/a" or boxed markdown.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





8. Open the same attack link of GitHub or GitLab in Firebox, and move your mouse over the payload. You can see the browser works fine and does not cause any trouble here.



<span class="line"><!---->8. Open the same attack link of GitHub or GitLab in Firebox, and move your mouse over the payload. You can see the browser works fine and does not cause any trouble here.<!----></span>



<br>

Problem Description:



<b class="line"><!---->Problem Description:<!----></b>



<br>





Google chrome is vulnerable to REDoS. Google chrome is incorrectly validating the Markdown function. GitHub and GitLab use markdown on their page to show the repository(README.md file) as beautiful. But if the attacker enters the malformed attribute in markdown, it leads the user to unaccessible the current chrome tab.



<span class="line"><!---->Google chrome is vulnerable to REDoS. Google chrome is incorrectly validating the Markdown function. GitHub and GitLab use markdown on their page to show the repository(README.md file) as beautiful. But if the attacker enters the malformed attribute in markdown, it leads the user to unaccessible the current chrome tab.<!----></span>



<br>





It renders all the payload characters in the <span> tag and consumes more memory and power of the system. But the issue is not present in the firebox. It only occurs in chromium-based systems. I had reported this issue to both Gitlab and Github, but their statement was " it is the browser's issue, chrome is vulnerable. And it only exists in chrome, not in firebox"



<span class="line"><!---->It renders all the payload characters in the &lt;span&gt; tag and consumes more memory and power of the system. But the issue is not present in the firebox. It only occurs in chromium-based systems. I had reported this issue to both Gitlab and Github, but their statement was " it is the browser's issue, chrome is vulnerable. And it only exists in chrome, not in firebox"<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

For markup both the "math"(Render mathematical expressions) and "Mermaid"(Mermaid lets you create diagrams and visualizations using text and code), attributes were used and it is rendered without causing any Tab level DosS. In my report, I made it with the "python" attribute. I will put the payload file (Payload.txt) in the attachment.

But here I'm using regular expression DoS causing the chrome tab( Tab with payload or Payloaded website opened in the tab)is not available for users who visit the page. So the payload is rendered in multiple "span" tags and consumes more memory and power of the user's device.

> Your team said DoS is not a security issue. But here I'm using regular expression DoS causing the chrome tab( Tab with payload or Payloaded website opened in the tab)is not available for users who visit the page. So the payload is rendered in multiple "span" tags and consumes more memory and power of the user's device. 



<span class="line"><!---->&gt; Your team said DoS is not a security issue. But here I'm using regular expression DoS causing the chrome tab( Tab with payload or Payloaded website opened in the tab)is not available for users who visit the page. So the payload is rendered in multiple "span" tags and consumes more memory and power of the user's device. <!----></span>



<br>



<br>

<h3 class="medium-heading"><!----> issue</h3>


          


            

Target project:

<label for="targetProjectInput">Target project:</label>


            


              

<input id="targetProjectInput" aria-owns="chops-autocomplete-1" aria-autocomplete="both" aria-expanded="false" aria-haspopup="listbox" aria-activedescendant="">


              




      


        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.
         */
        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr {
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr[data-selected] {
          background: var(--chops-active-choice-bg);
          text-decoration: underline;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container td {
          padding: 0.25em 8px;
          white-space: nowrap;
        }
        .screenreader-hidden {
          clip: rect(1px, 1px, 1px, 1px);
          height: 1px;
          overflow: hidden;
          position: absolute;
          white-space: nowrap;
          width: 1px;
        }
      

<style>
        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.
         */
        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr {
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr[data-selected] {
          background: var(--chops-active-choice-bg);
          text-decoration: underline;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container td {
          padding: 0.25em 8px;
          white-space: nowrap;
        }
        .screenreader-hidden {
          clip: rect(1px, 1px, 1px, 1px);
          height: 1px;
          overflow: hidden;
          position: absolute;
          white-space: nowrap;
          width: 1px;
        }
      </style>
